# Codebase Search Guide

Run these commands from the root of a cloned OpenWrt repository to find likely positive examples.

## build-system

```bash
grep -R \"uci commit|uci set|uci add_list\" package/
grep -R "/etc/config" package/
grep -R \"require view|require form|rpc.declare\" .
find . -path "*luci*" -name "*.js"
grep -R "EXTRA_CFLAGS" package/ target/
grep -R \"PKG_VERSION|PKG_SOURCE|PKG_HASH\" package/
grep -R \"procd_set_param|procd_open_instance|USE_PROCD\" package/
find package -path "*/files/*" -name "*.init"
grep -R \"bridge|vlan|firewall|netifd\" package/ target/
```

## concurrency

```bash
grep -R \"PKG_SOURCE_VERSION|backport|upstream\" package/
grep -R "ustream-openssl.c" .
grep -R "CMakeLists.txt" .
grep -R "dlink-sge-image.c" .
grep -R "dlink-sge-image.h" .
grep -R "EXTRA_CFLAGS" package/ target/
grep -R \"PKG_VERSION|PKG_SOURCE|PKG_HASH\" package/
grep -R \"uci commit|uci set|uci add_list\" package/
grep -R "/etc/config" package/
grep -R \"bridge|vlan|firewall|netifd\" package/ target/
grep -R "gpt.h" .
grep -R "image-commands.mk" .
grep -R "cgptlib_internal.h" .
grep -R "common.sh" .
grep -R "platform.sh" .
grep -R \"procd_set_param|procd_open_instance|USE_PROCD\" package/
find package -path "*/files/*" -name "*.init"
grep -R "mt7621_zyxel_lte3301-plus.dts" .
grep -R "mt7621.mk" .
grep -R "01_leds" .
grep -R "02_network" .
grep -R "ramips" .
grep -R "checkpatch.pl" .
grep -R "functions.sh" .
```

## kernel-driver

## luci-frontend

```bash
grep -R \"uci commit|uci set|uci add_list\" package/
grep -R "/etc/config" package/
grep -R \"require view|require form|rpc.declare\" .
find . -path "*luci*" -name "*.js"
grep -R "EXTRA_CFLAGS" package/ target/
grep -R \"PKG_VERSION|PKG_SOURCE|PKG_HASH\" package/
grep -R \"procd_set_param|procd_open_instance|USE_PROCD\" package/
find package -path "*/files/*" -name "*.init"
grep -R \"bridge|vlan|firewall|netifd\" package/ target/
grep -R "02-openwrt-prod.yml" .
grep -R \"PKG_SOURCE_VERSION|backport|upstream\" package/
grep -R "lantiq_dsl.sh" .
grep -R "100-dsl_compat.patch" .
grep -R "100-compat.patch" .
grep -R "Makefile" .
grep -R "dsl_control" .
grep -R \"malloc|calloc|realloc|free(\" package/ tools/
grep -R "pcre2*.h" .
grep -R "Config.in" .
grep -R "10_indicate_preinit" .
grep -R "config_generate" .
grep -R "boot" .

grep -R "80_mount_root" .
```

## memory-management

## package-packaging

```bash
grep -R \"uci commit|uci set|uci add_list\" package/
grep -R "/etc/config" package/
grep -R \"require view|require form|rpc.declare\" .
find . -path "*luci*" -name "*.js"
grep -R "EXTRA_CFLAGS" package/ target/
grep -R \"PKG_VERSION|PKG_SOURCE|PKG_HASH\" package/
grep -R \"procd_set_param|procd_open_instance|USE_PROCD\" package/
find package -path "*/files/*" -name "*.init"
grep -R \"bridge|vlan|firewall|netifd\" package/ target/
grep -R "02-openwrt-prod.yml" .
grep -R \"PKG_SOURCE_VERSION|backport|upstream\" package/
grep -R "gpt.h" .
grep -R "image-commands.mk" .
grep -R "cgptlib_internal.h" .
grep -R "common.sh" .
grep -R "platform.sh" .
grep -R "functions.sh" .
grep -R "10_rename_interfaces.sh" .
grep -R "qca9557_mikrotik_routerboard-960pgs.dts" .
grep -R "rbpoe.c" .
grep -R "rbpoe.h" .
grep -R "lantiq_dsl.sh" .
grep -R "100-dsl_compat.patch" .
grep -R "100-compat.patch" .
grep -R "Makefile" .
grep -R "dsl_control" .
grep -R \"malloc|calloc|realloc|free(\" package/ tools/
grep -R "pcre2*.h" .
grep -R "Config.in" .
grep -R "at91bootstrap.mk" .
grep -R "001-Makefile-Remove-nostartfiles-from-LDFLAGS.patch" .
```

## patch-maintenance

```bash
grep -R \"PKG_SOURCE_VERSION|backport|upstream\" package/
```
